0;\n+    var iter = std.unicode.Utf8View.initUnchecked(str).iterator();\n+    while (iter.nextCodepoint()) |cp| {\n+        width +|= cell_mod.Cell.charWidth(cp);\n+    }\n+    return for:\n+/// - Clearing a region before rendering a popup or overlay\n+/// - Drawing a solid background area\n+/// - Erasing content in a specific region\n+pub const Clear = struct {\n+    /// Style to fill the area with.\n+    /// The background color of this style determines the fill color.\n+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Character to fill with. render(self: Clear, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n+\n+        const fill_cell = Cell.styled(self.char, self.style);\n+        buf.fill(area, fill_cell);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Create a clear widget with a background color.\n+    pub fn withBackground(color: style_mod.Color) Clear {\n+        return .{\n+            .style = Style.init().bg(color),\n+        };\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic Clear functionality\n+// style\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+const buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\n+const geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\n+const style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n+\n+pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n+pub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\n+pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n+pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n+\n+/// Scrollbar orientation.\n+pub const Orientation = enum {\n+    vertical,\n+    horizontal,\n+};\n+\n+/// Scroll position indicator widget.\n+///\n+/// Displays a scrollbar track with a thumb indicating the current scroll position.\n+/// The thumb size is proportional to the viewport size relative to total content.\n+/// Supports both vertical and horizontal orientations.\n+pub const Scrollbar = struct {\n+    /// Total number of items/lines in the scrollable content.\n+    total: usize = 0,\n+\n+    /// Current scroll position (index of first visible item).\n+    position: usize = 0,\n+\n+    /// Number of items visible in the viewport.\n+    viewport: u16 = 0,\n+\n+    /// Style applied to the scrollbar track.\n+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Style applied to the scrollbar thumb.\n+    thumb_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n+\n+    /// Orientation of the scrollbar.\n+    orientation: Orientation = .vertical,\n+\n+    /// Characters used for rendering.\n+    /// Track character fills the scrollbar background.\n+    track_char: u21 = ' ',\n+\n+    /// Thumb character fills the scrollbar thumb.\n+    thumb_char: u21 = ' ',\n+\n+    /// Render the scrollbar into the buffer at the given area.\n+    pub fn render(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n+\n+        const track_length = switch (self.orientation) {\n+            .vertical => area.height,\n+            .horizontal => area.width,\n+        };\n+\n+        if (track_length == 0) return;\n+\n+        // Draw the track first\n+        self.drawTrack(area, buf);\n+\n+        // Calculate and draw the thumb\n+        if (self.total > 0 and self.viewport > 0) {\n+            const thumb_info = self.calculateThumb(track_length);\n+            self.drawThumb(area, thumb_info.start, thumb_info.length, buf);\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Draw the scrollbar track.\n+    fn drawTrack(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        const track_cell = Cell.styled(self.track_char, self.style);\n+\n+        switch (self.orientation) {\n+            .vertical => {\n+                var y = area.y;\n+                while (y < area.bottom()) : (y += 1) {\n+                    buf.set(area.x, y, track_cell);\n+                }\n+            },\n+            .horizontal => {\n+                var x = area.x;\n+                while (x < area.right()) : (x += 1) {\n+                    buf.set(x, area.y, track_cell);\n+                }\n+            },\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Draw the scrollbar thumb at the calculated position.\n+    fn drawThumb(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, start: u16, length: u16, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (length == 0) return;\n+\n+        const thumb_cell = Cell.styled(self.thumb_char, self.thumb_style);\n+\n+        switch (self.orientation) {\n+            .vertical => {\n+                const thumb_y = area.y +| start;\n+                var y = thumb_y;\n+                while (y < thumb_y +| length and y < area.bottom()) : (y += 1) {\n+                    buf.set(area.x, y, thumb_cell);\n+                }\n+            },\n+            .horizontal => {\n+                const thumb_x = area.x +| start;\n+                var x = thumb_x;\n+                while (x < thumb_x +| length and x < area.right()) : (x += 1) {\n+                    buf.set(x, area.y, thumb_cell);\n+                }\n+            },\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Calculate thumb position and size.\n+    fn calculateThumb(self: Scrollbar, track_length: u16) struct { start: u16, length: u16 } {\n+        if (self.total == 0 or self.viewport == 0 or track_length == 0) {\n+            return .{ .start = 0, .length = 0 };\n+        }\n+\n+        const total_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.total);\n+        const viewport_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.viewport);\n+        const track_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(track_length);\n+        const position_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.position);\n+\n+        // Thumb length proportional to viewport/total ratio\n+        const thumb_ratio = @min(viewport_f / total_f, 1.0);\n+        var thumb_length: u16 = @intFromFloat(@max(thumb_ratio * track_f, 1.0));\n+        thumb_length = @min(thumb_length, track_length);\n+\n+        // Thumb position based on scroll position\n+        const scrollable_items = if (self.total > self.viewport)\n+            self.total - self.viewport\n+        else\n+            0;\n+\n+        var thumb_start: u16 = 0;\n+        if (scrollable_items > 0) {\n+            const scrollable_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(scrollable_items);\n+            const scrollable_track = track_length -| thumb_length;\n+            const scrollable_track_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(scrollable_track);\n+\n+            const position_ratio = @min(position_f / scrollable_f, 1.0);\n+            thumb_start = @intFromFloat(position_ratio * scrollable_track_f);\n+        }\n+\n+        return .{ .start = thumb_start, .length = thumb_length };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Create a scrollbar for a list with the given state.\n+    pub fn forList(items_count: usize, selected: usize, visible_rows: u16) Scrollbar {\n+        return .{\n+            .total = items_count,\n+            .position = selected,\n+            .viewport = visible_rows,\n+        };\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic Scrollbar functionality\n+// 0000000..e7fc2df\n--- /dev/null\n+++ b/src/widgets/scrollbar.zig\n@@ -0,0 +1,408 @@\n+// Scrollbar widget for zithril TUI framework\n+// Scroll position indicator with configurable orientation and style\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+const buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\n+const geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\n+const style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n+\n+pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n+pub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\n+pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n+pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n+\n+/// Scrollbar orientation.\n+pub const Orientation = enum {\n+    vertical,\n+    horizontal,\n+};\n+\n+/// Scroll position indicator widget.\n+///\n+/// Displays a scrollbar track with a thumb indicating the current scroll position.\n+/// The thumb size is proportional to the viewport size relative to total content.\n+/// Supports both vertical and horizontal orientations.\n+pub const Scrollbar = struct {\n+    /// Total number of items/lines in the scrollable content.\n+    total: usize = 0,\n+\n+    /// Current scroll position (index of first visible item).\n+    position: usize = 0,\n+\n+    /// Number of items visible in the viewport.\n+    viewport: u16 = 0,\n+\n+    /// Style applied to the scrollbar track.\n+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Style applied to the scrollbar thumb.\n+    thumb_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n+\n+    /// Orientation of the scrollbar.\n+    orientation: Orientation = .vertical,\n+\n+    /// Characters used for rendering.\n+    /// Track character fills the scrollbar background.\n+    track_char: u21 = ' ',\n+\n+    /// Thumb character fills the scrollbar thumb.\n+    thumb_char: u21 = ' ',\n+\n+    /// Render the scrollbar into the buffer at the given area.\n+    pub fn render(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n+\n+        const track_length = switch (self.orientation) {\n+            .vertical => area.height,\n+            .horizontal => area.width,\n+        };\n+\n+        if (track_length == 0) return;\n+\n+        // Draw the track first\n+        self.drawTrack(area, buf);\n+\n+        // Calculate and draw the thumb\n+        if (self.total > 0 and self.viewport > 0) {\n+            const thumb_info = self.calculateThumb(track_length);\n+            self.drawThumb(area, thumb_info.start, thumb_info.length, buf);\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Draw the scrollbar track.\n+    fn drawTrack(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        const track_cell = Cell.styled(self.track_char, self.style);\n+\n+        switch (self.orientation) {\n+            .vertical => {\n+                var y = area.y;\n+                while (y < area.bottom()) : (y += 1) {\n+                    buf.set(area.x, y, track_cell);\n+                }\n+            },\n+            .horizontal => {\n+                var x = area.x;\n+                while (x < area.right()) : (x += 1) {\n+                    buf.set(x, area.y, track_cell);\n+                }\n+            },\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Draw the scrollbar thumb at the calculated position.\n+    fn drawThumb(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, start: u16, length: u16, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (length == 0) return;\n+\n+        const thumb_cell = Cell.styled(self.thumb_char, self.thumb_style);\n+\n+        switch (self.orientation) {\n+            .vertical => {\n+                const thumb_y = area.y +| start;\n+                var y = thumb_y;\n+                while (y < thumb_y +| length and y < area.bottom()) : (y += 1) {\n+                    buf.set(area.x, y, thumb_cell);\n+                }\n+            },\n+            .horizontal => {\n+                const thumb_x = area.x +| start;\n+                var x = thumb_x;\n+                while (x < thumb_x +| length and x < area.right()) : (x += 1) {\n+                    buf.set(x, area.y, thumb_cell);\n+                }\n+            },\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Calculate thumb position and size.\n+    fn calculateThumb(self: Scrollbar, track_length: u16) struct { start: u16, length: u16 } {\n+        if (self.total == 0 or self.viewport == 0 or track_length == 0) {\n+            return .{ .start = 0, .length = 0 };\n+        }\n+\n+        const total_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.total);\n+        const viewport_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.viewport);\n+        const track_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(track_length);\n+        const position_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.position);\n+\n+        // Thumb length proportional to viewport/total ratio\n+        const thumb_ratio = @min(viewport_f / total_f, 1.0);\n+        var thumb_length: u16 = @intFromFloat(@max(thumb_ratio * track_f, 1.0));\n+        thumb_length = @min(thumb_length, track_length);\n+\n+        // Thumb position based on scroll position\n+        const scrollable_items = if (self.total > self.viewport)\n+            self.total - self.viewport\n+        else\n+            0;\n+\n+        var thumb_start: u16 = 0;\n+        if (scrollable_items > 0) {\n+            const scrollable_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(scrollable_items);\n+            const scrollable_track = track_length -| thumb_length;\n+            const scrollable_track_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(scrollable_track);\n+\n+            const position_ratio = @min(position_f / scrollable_f, 1.0);\n+            thumb_start = @intFromFloat(position_ratio * scrollable_track_f);\n+        }\n+\n+        return .{ .start = thumb_start, .length = thumb_length };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Create a scrollbar for a list with the given state.\n+    pub fn forList(items_count: usize, selected: usize, visible_rows: u16) Scrollbar {\n+        return .{\n+            .total = items_count,\n+            .position = selected,\n+            .viewport = visible_rows,\n+        };\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic Scrollbar functionality\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"sanity: Scrollbar with default values\" {\n+    const scrollbar = Scrollbar{};\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), scrollbar.total);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), scrollbar.position);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 0), scrollbar.viewport);\n+    try std.testing.expect(scrollbar.orientation == .vertical);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Scrollbar with values\" {\n+    const scrollbar = Scrollbar{\n+        .total = 100,\n+        .position = 25,\n+ u16 } {\n   118        if (self.total == 0 or self.viewport == 0 or track_length == 0) {\n   119            return .{ .start = 0, .length = 0 };\n   120        }\n   121\n   122        const total_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.total);\n   123        const viewport_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.viewport);\n   124        const track_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(track_length);\n   125        const position_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.position);\n   126\n   127        // Thumb length proportional to viewport/total ratio\n   128        const thumb_ratio = @min(viewport_f / total_f, 1.0);\n   129        var thumb_length: u16 = @intFromFloat(@max(thumb_ratio * track_f, 1.0));\n   130        thumb_length = @min(thumb_length, track_length);\n   131\n   132        // Thumb position based on scroll position\n   133        const scrollable_items = if (self.total > self.viewport)\n   134            self.total - self.viewport\n   135        else\n   136            0;\n   137\n   138        var thumb_start: u16 = 0;\n   139        if (scrollable_items > 0) {\n   140            const scrollable_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(scrollable_items);\n   141            const scrollable_track = track_length -| thumb_length;\n   142            const scrollable_track_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(scrollable_track);\n   143\n   144            const position_ratio = @min(position_f / scrollable_f, 1.0);\n   145            thumb_start = @intFromFloat(position_ratio * scrollable_track_f);\n   146        }\n   147\n   148        return .{ .start = thumb_start, .length = thumb_length };\n   149    }\n   150\n   151    /// Create a scrollbar for a list with the given state.\n   152    pub fn forList(items_count: usize, selected: usize, visible_rows: u16) Scrollbar {\n   153        return .{\n   154            .total = items_count,\n   155            .position = selected,\n   156            .viewport = visible_rows,\n   157        };\n   158    }\n   159};\n   160\n   161// Scrollbar widget for zithril TUI framework\n// Scroll position indicator with configurable orientation and style\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\nconst geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\nconst style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n\npub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\npub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\npub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\npub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n\n/// Scrollbar orientation.\npub const Orientation = enum {\n    vertical,\n    horizontal,\n};\n\n/// Scroll position indicator widget.\n///\n/// Displays a scrollbar track with a thumb indicating the current scroll position.\n/// The thumb size is proportional to the viewport size relative to total content.\n/// Supports both vertical and horizontal orientations.\npub const Scrollbar = struct {\n    /// Total number of items/lines in the scrollable content.\n    total: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Current scroll position (index of first visible item).\n    position: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Number of items visible in the viewport.\n    viewport: u16 = 0,\n\n    /// Style applied to the scrollbar track.\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Style applied to the scrollbar thumb.\n    thumb_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n\n    /// Orientation of the scrollbar.\n    orientation: Orientation = .vertical,\n\n    /// Characters used for rendering.\n    /// Track character fills the scrollbar background.\n    track_char: u21 = ' ',\n\n    /// Thumb character fills the scrollbar thumb.\n    thumb_char: u21 = ' ',\n\n    /// Render the scrollbar into the buffer at the given area.\n    pub fn render(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n\n        const track_length = switch (self.orientation) {\n            .vertical => area.height,\n            .horizontal => area.width,\n        };\n\n        if (track_length == 0) return;\n\n        // Draw the track first\n        self.drawTrack(area, buf);\n\n        // Calculate and draw the thumb\n        if (self.total > 0 and self.viewport > 0) {\n            const thumb_info = self.calculateThumb(track_length);\n            self.drawThumb(area, thumb_info.start, thumb_info.length, buf);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Draw the scrollbar track.\n    fn drawTrack(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        const track_cell = Cell.styled(self.track_char, self.style);\n\n        switch (self.orientation) {\n            .vertical => {\n                var y = area.y;\n                while (y < area.bottom()) : (y += 1) {\n                    buf.set(area.x, y, track_cell);\n                }\n            },\n            .horizontal => {\n                var x = area.x;\n                while (x < area.right()) : (x += 1) {\n                    buf.set(x, area.y, track_cell);\n                }\n            },\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Draw the scrollbar thumb at the calculated position.\n    fn drawThumb(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, start: u16, length: u16, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (length == 0) return;\n\n        const thumb_cell = Cell.styled(self.thumb_char, self.thumb_style);\n\n        switch (self.orientation) {\n            .vertical => {\n                const thumb_y = area.y +| start;\n                var y = thumb_y;\n                while (y < thumb_y +| length and y < area.bottom()) : (y += 1) {\n                    buf.set(area.x, y, thumb_cell);\n                }\n            },\n            .horizontal => {\n                const thumb_x = area.x +| start;\n                var x = thumb_x;\n                while (x < thumb_x +| length and x < area.right()) : (x += 1) {\n                    buf.set(x, area.y, thumb_cell);\n                }\n            },\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Calculate thumb position and size.\n    fn calculateThumb(self: Scrollbar, track_length: u16) struct { start: u16, length: u16 } {\n        if (self.total == 0 or self.viewport == 0 or track_length == 0) {\n            return .{ .start = 0, .length = 0 };\n        }\n\n        const total_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.total);\n        const viewport_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.viewport);\n        const track_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(track_length);\n        const position_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.position);\n\n        // Thumb length proportional to viewport/total ratio\n        const thumb_ratio = @min(viewport_f / total_f, 1.0);\n        var thumb_length: u16 = @intFromFloat(@max(thumb_ratio * track_f, 1.0));\n        thumb_length = @min(thumb_length, track_length);\n\n        // Thumb position based on scroll position\n        const scrollable_items = if (self.total > self.viewport)\n            self.total - self.viewport\n        else\n            0;\n\n        var thumb_start: u16 = 0;\n        if (scrollable_items > 0) {\n            const scrollable_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(scrollable_items);\n            const scrollable_track = track_length -| thumb_length;\n            const scrollable_track_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(scrollable_track);\n\n            const position_ratio = @min(position_f / scrollable_f, 1.0);\n            thumb_start = @intFromFloat(position_ratio * scrollable_track_f);\n        }\n\n        return .{ .start = thumb_start, .length = thumb_length };\n    }\n\n    /// Create a scrollbar for a list with the given state.\n    pub fn forList(items_count: usize, selected: usize, visible_rows: u16) Scrollbar {\n        return .{\n            .total = items_count,\n            .position = selected,\n            .viewport = visible_rows,\n        };\n    }\n};\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - Basic Scrollbar functionality\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"sanity: Scrollbar with default values\" {\n    const scrollbar = Scrollbar{};\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), scrollbar.total);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), scrollbar.position);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 0), scrollbar.viewport);\n    try std.testing.expect(scrollbar.orientation == .vertical);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Scrollbar with values\" {\n    const scrollbar = Scrollbar{\n        .total = 100,\n        .position = 25,\n        .viewport = 10,\n        .orientation = .horizontal,\n    };\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 100), scrollbar.total);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 25), scrollbar.position);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 10), scrollbar.viewport);\n    try std.testing.expect(scrollbar.orientation == .horizontal);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Scrollbar.forList creates correctly\" {\n {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01EU1iyCCbNQnHdMeBjxxw7G","type":"tool_result","content":"     1// Paragraph widget for zithril TUI framework\n     2// Multi-line text with wrapping and alignment\n     3\n     4const std = @import(\"std\");\n     5const buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\n     6const geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\n     7const style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n     8const text_mod = @import(\"../text.zig\");\n     9\n    10pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n    11pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n    12pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n    13\n    14/// Text wrapping modes\n    15pub const Wrap = enum {\n    16    /// No wrapping, clip at boundary\n    17    none,\n    18    /// Wrap at any character position\n    19    char,\n    20    /// Wrap at word boundaries (spaces)\n    21    word,\n    22};\n    23\n    24/// Text alignment options\n    25pub const Alignment = enum {\n    26    left,\n    27    center,\n    28    right,\n    29};\n    30\n    31/// Multi-line text widget with optional wrapping.\n    32///\n    33/// Renders text content across multiple lines with configurable wrapping\n    34/// behavior and alignment. Lines beyond the area height are not rendered.\n    35pub const Paragraph = struct {\n    36    /// The text content to display\n    37    text: []const u8,\n    38\n    39    /// Style applied to the text\n    40    style: Style = Style.empty,\n    41\n    42    /// Text wrapping mode\n    43    wrap: Wrap = .none,\n    44\n    45    /// Text alignment within each line\n    46    alignment: Alignment = .left,\n    47\n    48    /// Render the paragraph into the buffer at the given area.\n    49    /// Text is split into lines (either by newlines or wrapping) and rendered\n    50    /// until the area height is filled.\n    51    pub fn render(self: Paragraph, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n    52        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n    53        if (self.text.len == 0) return;\n    54\n    55        var y = area.y;\n    56        const max_y = area.bottom();\n    57\n    58        // Process text line by line (split by newlines first)\n    59        var line_iter = std.mem.splitScalar(u8, self.text, '\\n');\n    60        while (line_iter.next()) |logical_line| {\n    61            if (y >= max_y) break;\n    62\n    63            // Apply wrapping to this logical line\n    64            switch (self.wrap) {\n    65                .none => {\n    66                    self.renderLine(logical_line, area.x, y, area.width, buf);\n    67                    y += 1;\n    68                },\n    69                .char => {\n    70                    var remaining = logical_line;\n    71                    while (remaining.len > 0 and y < max_y) {\n    72                        const chunk_len = @min(remaining.len, area.width);\n    73                        const chunk = remaining[0..chunk_len];\n    74                        self.renderLine(chunk, area.x, y, area.width, buf);\n    75                        remaining = remaining[chunk_len..];\n    76                        y += 1;\n    77                    }\n    78                    // Empty line should still take a row\n    79                    if (logical_line.len == 0) {\n    80                        y += 1;\n    81                    }\n    82                },\n    83                .word => {\n    84                    if (logical_line.len == 0) {\n    85                        y += 1;\n    86                        continue;\n    87                    }\n    88                    var line_start: usize = 0;\n    89                    while (line_start < logical_line.len and y < max_y) {\n    90                        const wrap_end = findWordWrapEnd(logical_line[line_start..], area.width);\n    91                        const line = logical_line[line_start .. line_start + wrap_end];\n    92                        self.renderLine(line, area.x, y, area.width, buf);\n    93                        line_start += wrap_end;\n    94                        // Skip leading spaces on next line\n    95                        while (line_start < logical_line.len and logical_line[line_start] == ' ') {\n    96                            line_start += 1;\n    97                        }\n    98                        y += 1;\n    99                    }\n   100                },\n   101            }\n   102        }\n   103    }\n   104\n   105    /// Render a single line of text with alignment\n   106    fn renderLine(self: Paragraph, line: []const u8, x: u16, y: u16, width: u16, buf: *Buffer) void {\n   107        if (line.len == 0) return;\n   108\n   109        const text_len = text_mod.displayWidth(line);\n   110        const visible_len = @min(text_len, width);\n   111\n   112        if (visible_len == 0) return;\n   113\n   114        const x_offset: u16 = switch (self.alignment) {\n   115            .left => 0,\n   116            .center => (width -| visible_len) / 2,\n   117            .right => width -| visible_len,\n   118        };\n   119\n   120        buf.setString(x +| x_offset, y, line, self.style);\n   121    }\n   122};\n   123\n   124/// Find the end index for word wrapping within a max width.\n   125/// Returns the number of characters to include on this line.\n   126fn findWordWrapEnd(text: []const u8, max_width: u16) usize {\n   127    if (text.len == 0) return 0;\n   128\n   129    const width: usize = @intCast(max_width);\n   130    if (text.len <= width) return text.len;\n   131\n   132    // Find the last space within the width limit\n   133    var last_space: ?usize = null;\n   134    for (0..width) |i| {\n   135        if (text[i] == ' ') {\n   136            last_space = i;\n   137        }\n   138    }\n   139\n   140    // If we found a space, wrap there (include the space in this line)\n   141    if (last_space) |space_pos| {\n   142        // Return position including the space, so next line starts after it\n   143        return space_pos + 1;\n   144    }\n   145\n   146    // No space found - break at max width (hard wrap)\n   147    return width;\n   148}\n   149\n   150\n   151// ============================================================\n   152// SANITY TESTS - Basic Paragraph functionality\n   153// ============================================================\n   154\n   155test \"sanity: Paragraph with default values\" {\n   156    const para = Paragraph{ .text = \"Hello\\nWorld\" };\n   157    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"Hello\\nWorld\", para.text);\n   158    try std.testing.expect(para.style.isEmpty());\n   159    try std.testing.expect(para.wrap == .none);\n   160    try std.testing.expect(para.alignment == .left);\n   161}\n   162\n   163test \"sanity: Paragraph with custom style\" {\n   164    const para = Paragraph{\n   165        .text = \"Styled\",\n   166        .style = Style.init().bold().fg(.red),\n   167    };\n   168    try std.testing.expect(para.style.hasAttribute(.bold));\n   169}\n   170\n   171test \"sanity: Paragraph with wrap modes\" {\n   172 179}\n   180\n   181test \"sanity: Paragraph with alignment\" {\n   182    const left = Paragraph{ .text = \"L\", .alignment = .left };\n   183    const center = Paragraph{ .text = \"C\", .alignment = .center };\n   184    const right = Paragraph{ .text = \"R\", .alignment = .right };\n   185\n   186    try std.testing.expect(left.alignment == .left);\n   187    try std.testing.expect(center.alignment == .center);\n   188    try std.testing.expect(right.alignment == .right);\n   189}\n   190\n   191// ============================================================\n Lines beyond the area height are not rendered.\npub const Paragraph = struct {\n    /// The text content to display\n    text: []const u8,\n\n    /// Style applied to the text\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Text wrapping mode\n    wrap: Wrap = .none,\n\n    /// Text alignment within each line\n    alignment: Alignment = .left,\n\n    /// Render the paragraph into the buffer at the given area.\n    /// Text is split into lines (either by newlines or wrapping) and rendered\n    /// until the area height is filled.\n    pub fn render(self: Paragraph, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n        if (self.text.len == 0) return;\n\n        var y = area.y;\n        const max_y = area.bottom();\n\n        // Process text line by line (split by newlines first)\n        var line_iter = std.mem.splitScalar(u8, self.text, '\\n');\n        while (line_iter.next()) |logical_line| {\n            if (y >= max_y) break;\n\n            // Apply wrapping to this logical line\n            switch (self.wrap) {\n                .none => {\n                    self.renderLine(logical_line, area.x, y, area.width, buf);\n                    y += 1;\n                },\n                .char => {\n                    var remaining = logical_line;\n                    while (remaining.len > 0 and y < max_y) {\n                        const chunk_len = @min(remaining.len, area.width);\n                        const chunk = remaining[0..chunk_len];\n                        self.renderLine(chunk, area.x, y, area.width, buf);\n                        remaining = remaining[chunk_len..];\n                        y += 1;\n                    }\n                    // Empty line should still take a row\n                    if (logical_line.len == 0) {\n                        y += 1;\n                    }\n                },\n                .word => {\n                    if (logical_line.len == 0) {\n                        y += 1;\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                    var line_start: usize = 0;\n                    while (line_start < logical_line.len and y < max_y) {\n                        const wrap_end = findWordWrapEnd(logical_line[line_start..], area.width);\n                        const line = logical_line[line_start .. line_start + wrap_end];\n                        self.renderLine(line, area.x, y, area.width, buf);\n                        line_start += wrap_end;\n                        // Skip leading spaces on next line\n                        while (line_start < logical_line.len and logical_line[line_start] == ' ') {\n                            line_start += 1;\n                        }\n                        y += 1;\n                    }\n                },\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Render a single line of text with alignment\n    fn renderLine(self: Paragraph, line: []const u8, x: u16, y: u16, width: u16, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (line.len == 0) return;\n\n        const text_len = text_mod.displayWidth(line);\n        const visible_len = @min(text_len, width);\n\n        if (visible_len == 0) return;\n\n        const x_offset: u16 = switch (self.alignment) {\n            .left => 0,\n            .center => (width -| visible_len) / 2,\n            .right => width -| visible_len,\n        };\n\n        buf.setString(x +| x_offset, y, line, self.style);\n    }\n};\n\n/// Find the end index for word wrapping within a max width.\n/// Returns the number of characters to include on this line.\nfn findWordWrapEnd(text: []const u8, max_width: u16) usize {\n    if (text.len == 0) return 0;\n\n    const width: usize = @intCast(max_width);\n    if (text.len <= width) return text.len;\n\n    // Find the last space within the width limit\n    var last_space: ?usize = null;\n    for (0..width) |i| {\n        if (text[i] == ' ') {\n            last_space = i;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we found a space, wrap there (include the space in this line)\n    if (last_space) |space_pos| {\n        // Return position including the space, so next line starts after it\n        return space_pos + 1;\n    }\n\n    // No space found - break at max width (hard wrap)\n    return width;\n}\n\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - Basic Paragraph functionality\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"sanity: Paragraph with default values\" {\n    const para = Paragraph{ .text = \"Hello\\nWorld\" };\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"Hello\\nWorld\", para.text);\n    try std.testing.expect(para.style.isEmpty());\n    try std.testing.expect(para.wrap == .none);\n    try std.testing.expect(para.alignment == .left);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Paragraph with custom style\" {\n    const para = Paragraph{\n        .text = \"Styled\",\n        .style = Style.init().bold().fg(.red),\n    };\n    try std.testing.expect(para.style.hasAttribute(.bold));\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Paragraph with wrap modes\" {\n    const none_wrap = Paragraph{ .text = \"T\", .wrap = .none };\n    const char_wrap = Paragraph{ .text = \"T\", .wrap = .char };\n    const word_wrap = Paragraph{ .text = \"T\", .wrap = .word };\n\n    try std.testing.expect(none_wrap.wrap == .none);\n    try std.testing.expect(char_wrap.wrap == .char);\n    try std.testing.expect(word_wrap.wrap == .word);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Paragraph with alignment\" {\n    const left = Paragraph{ .text = \"L\", .alignment = .left };\n    const center = Paragraph{ .text = \"C\", .alignment = .center };\n    const right = Paragraph{ .text = \"R\", .alignment = .right };\n\n    try std.testing.expect(left.alignment == .left);\n    try std.testing.expect(center.alignment == .center);\n    try std.testing.expect(right.alignment == .right);\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Rendering\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: Paragraph renders single line\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 5);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    const para = Paragraph{ .text = \"Hello\" };\n    para.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 5), &buf);\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'H'), buf.get(0, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'e'), buf.get(1, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'l'), @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\nconst style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\nconst text_mod = @import(\"../text.zig\");\n\npub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\npub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\npub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\npub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n\n/// Tabs widget displaying a horizontal tab bar.\n///\n/// Renders a row of tab titles with the selected tab highlighted.\n/// Tabs are separated by a configurable divider string.\npub const Tabs = struct {\n    /// Tab titles to display\n    titles: []const []const u8,\n\n    /// Index of the currently selected tab\n    selected: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Default style for unselected tabs\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Style for the selected tab\n    highlight_style: Style = Style.init().bold().fg(.yellow),\n\n    /// Divider string between tabs\n    divider: []const u8 = \" | \",\n\n    /// Render the tabs into the buffer at the given area.\n    /// Tabs are rendered horizontally on the first row of the area.\n    pub fn render(self: Tabs, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n        if (self.titles.len == 0) return;\n\n        var x = area.x;\n\n        for (self.titles, 0..) |title, idx| {\n            if (x >= area.right()) break;\n\n            // Determine if this tab is selected\n            const is_selected = idx == self.selected;\n            const tab_style = if (is_selected) self.highlight_style else self.style;\n\n            // Render tab title\n            const available_width = area.right() -| x;\n            if (available_width == 0) break;\n\n            const title_len = text_mod.displayWidth(title);\n            const render_len = @min(title_len, available_width);\n\n            if (render_len > 0) {\n                buf.setString(x, area.y, title, tab_style);\n            }\n\n            x +|= @intCast(render_len);\n\n            // Render divider after tab (except for last tab)\n            if (idx + 1 < self.titles.len and x < area.right()) {\n                const divider_available = area.right() -| x;\n                const divider_len = text_mod.displayWidth(self.divider);\n                const divider_render_len = @min(divider_len, divider_available);\n\n                if (divider_render_len > 0) {\n                    buf.setString(x, area.y, self.divider, self.style);\n                }\n\n                x +|= @intCast(divider_render_len);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get the number of tabs\n    pub fn count(self: Tabs) usize {\n        return self.titles.len;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if tabs are empty\n    pub fn isEmpty(self: Tabs) bool {\n        return self.titles.len == 0;\n    }\n\n    /// Get the selected tab index, clamped to valid range\n    pub fn selectedClamped(self: Tabs) ?usize {\n        if (self.titles.len == 0) return null;\n        return @min(self.selected, self.titles.len - 1);\n    }\n};\n\n\n// ============================================================\n// \"Tab2\", \"Tab3\" };\n    const tabs = Tabs{ .titles = &titles };\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 3), tabs.count());\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), tabs.selected);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\" | \", tabs.divider);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Tabs with selection\" {\n    const titles = [_][]const u8{ \"A\", \"B\", \"C\" };\n    const tabs = Tabs{\n };\n\n    try std.testing.expect(!tabs.style.isEmpty());\n    try std.testing.expect(tabs.highlight_style.hasAttribute(.bold));\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\" - \", tabs.divider);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Tabs.count and Tabs.isEmpty\" {\n    const titles = [_][]const u8{ \"A\", \"B\" };\n    const tabs = Tabs{ .titles = &titles };\n\n    try };\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), empty_tabs.count());\n    try std.testing.expect(empty_tabs.isEmpty());\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Tabs.selectedClamped\" {\n    const titles = [_][]const u8{ \"A\", \"B\" };\n    const tabs = Tabs{\n        .titles = &titles,\n        .selected = 5,\n    };\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(?usize, 1), tabs.selectedClamped());\n\n    const empty_titles = [_][]const u8{};\n    const empty_tabs = Tabs{ .titles = &empty_titles };\n\n    try std.testing.expect(empty_tabs.selectedClamped() == null);\n}\n\n// {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 30, 3);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    const titles = [_][]const u8{ \"One\", \"Two\", \"Three\" };\n    const tabs = Tabs{\n        .titles = Lines beyond the area height are not rendered.\npub const Paragraph = struct {\n    /// The text content to display\n    text: []const u8,\n\n    /// Style applied to the text\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Text wrapping mode\n    wrap: Wrap = .none,\n\n    /// Text alignment within each line\n    alignment: Alignment = .left,\n\n    /// Render the paragraph into the buffer at the given area.\n    /// Text is split into lines (either by newlines or wrapping) and rendered\n    /// until the area height is filled.\n    pub fn render(self: Paragraph, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n        if (self.text.len == 0) return;\n\n        var y = area.y;\n        const max_y = area.bottom();\n\n        // Process text line by line (split by newlines first)\n        var line_iter = std.mem.splitScalar(u8, self.text, '\\n');\n        while (line_iter.next()) |logical_line| {\n            if (y >= max_y) break;\n\n            // Apply wrapping to this logical line\n            switch (self.wrap) {\n                .none => {\n                    self.renderLine(logical_line, area.x, y, area.width, buf);\n                    y += 1;\n                },\n                .char => {\n                    var remaining = logical_line;\n                    while (remaining.len > 0 and y < max_y) {\n                        const chunk_len = @min(remaining.len, area.width);\n                        const chunk = remaining[0..chunk_len];\n                        self.renderLine(chunk, area.x, y, area.width, buf);\n                        remaining = remaining[chunk_len..];\n                        y += 1;\n                    }\n                    // Empty line should still take a row\n                    if (logical_line.len == 0) {\n                        y += 1;\n                    }\n                },\n                .word => {\n                    if (logical_line.len == 0) {\n                        y += 1;\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                    var line_start: usize = 0;\n                    while (line_start < logical_line.len and y < max_y) {\n                        const wrap_end = findWordWrapEnd(logical_line[line_start..], area.width);\n                        const line = logical_line[line_start .. line_start + wrap_end];\n                        self.renderLine(line, area.x, y, area.width, buf);\n                        line_start += wrap_end;\n                        // Skip leading spaces on next line\n                        while (line_start < logical_line.len and logical_line[line_start] == ' ') {\n                            line_start += 1;\n                        }\n                        y += 1;\n                    }\n                },\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Render a single line of text with alignment\n    fn renderLine(self: Paragraph, line: []const u8, x: u16, y: u16, width: u16, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (line.len == 0) return;\n\n        const text_len = text_mod.displayWidth(line);\n        const visible_len = @min(text_len, width);\n\n        if (visible_len == 0) return;\n\n        const x_offset: u16 = switch (self.alignment) {\n            .left => 0,\n            .center => (width -| visible_len) / 2,\n            .right => width -| visible_len,\n        };\n\n        buf.setString(x +| x_offset, y, line, self.style);\n    }\n};\n\n/// Find the end index for word wrapping within a max width.\n/// Returns the number of characters to include on this line.\nfn findWordWrapEnd(text: []const u8, max_width: u16) usize {\n    if (text.len == 0) return 0;\n\n    const width: usize = @intCast(max_width);\n    if (text.len <= width) return text.len;\n\n    // Find the last space within the width limit\n    var last_space: ?usize = null;\n    for (0..width) |i| {\n        if (text[i] == ' ') {\n            last_space = i;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we found a space, wrap there (include the space in this line)\n    if (last_space) |space_pos| {\n        // Return position including the space, so next line starts after it\n        return space_pos + 1;\n    }\n\n    // No space found - break at max width (hard wrap)\n    return width;\n}\n\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - Basic Paragraph functionality\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"sanity: Paragraph with default values\" {\n    const para = Paragraph{ .text = \"Hello\\nWorld\" };\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"Hello\\nWorld\", para.text);\n    try std.testing.expect(para.style.isEmpty());\n    try std.testing.expect(para.wrap == .none);\n    try std.testing.expect(para.alignment == .left);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Paragraph with custom style\" {\n    const para = Paragraph{\n        .text = \"Styled\",\n        .style = Style.init().bold().fg(.red),\n    };\n    try std.testing.expect(para.style.hasAttribute(.bold));\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Paragraph with wrap modes\" {\n    const none_wrap = Paragraph{ .text = \"T\", .wrap = .none };\n    const char_wrap = Paragraph{ .text = \"T\", .wrap = .char };\n    const word_wrap = Paragraph{ .text = \"T\", .wrap = .word };\n\n    try std.testing.expect(none_wrap.wrap == .none);\n    try std.testing.expect(char_wrap.wrap == .char);\n    try std.testing.expect(word_wrap.wrap == .word);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Paragraph with alignment\" {\n    const left = Paragraph{ .text = \"L\", .alignment = .left };\n    const center = Paragraph{ .text = \"C\", .alignment = .center };\n    const right = Paragraph{ .text = \"R\", .alignment = .right };\n\n    try std.testing.expect(left.alignment == .left);\n    try std.testing.expect(center.alignment == .center);\n    try std.testing.expect(right.alignment == .right);\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Rendering\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: Paragraph renders single line\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 5);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    const para = Paragraph{ .text = \"Hello\" };\n    para.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 5), &buf);\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'H'), buf.get(0, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'e'), buf.get(1, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'l'), buf.get(2, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'l'), buf.get(3, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'o'), buf.get(4, 0).char);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: Paragraph renders multiple lines with newlines\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 5);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    const para = Paragraph{ .text = \"Line1\\nLine2\\nLine3\" };\n    para.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 5), &buf);\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'L'), buf.get(0, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, '1'), buf.get(4, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'L'), buf.get(0, 1).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, '2'), buf.get(4, 1).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'L'), buf.get(0, 2).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, '3'), buf.get(4, 2).char);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: Paragraph with char wrap\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 10, 5);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    const para = Paragraph{\n        .text = \"ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOP\",\n        .wrap = .char,\n    };\n    para.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 10, 5), &buf);\n\n    // First 10 chars on row 0\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'A'), buf.get(0, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'J'), buf.get(9, 0).char);\n    // Next 6 chars on row 1\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'K'), buf.get(0, 1).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'P'), buf.get(5, 1).char);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: Paragraph with word wrap\" {\n    var buf = try // \"World \" should be on row 1\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'W'), buf.get(0, 1).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'd'), buf.get(4, 1).char);\n    // \"Today\" should be on row 2\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'T'), buf.get(0, 2).char);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: Paragraph center alignment\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 5);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    const para = Paragraph{\n        .text = \"Hi\",\n        .alignment = .center,\n    };\n    para.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 5), &buf);\n\n    // \"Hi\" (2 chars) centered in 20 = offset 9\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'H'), buf.get(9, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'i'), buf.get(10, 0).char);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: Paragraph right empty area\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 10, 10);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    const para = Paragraph{ .text = \"Test\" };\n    para.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 0, 0), unchanged\n    for (buf.cells) |cell| {\n        try std.testing.expect(cell.isDefault());\n    }\n}\n\ntest \"regression: Paragraph clips lines beyond height\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 2);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    const para = Paragraph{ .text = \"Line1\\nLine2\\nLine3\\nLine4\" };\n    para.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 2), &buf);\n\n    // Only first 2 lines should be rendered\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'L'), buf.get(0, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, '1'), buf.get(4, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'L'), buf.get(0, 1).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, '2'), buf.get(4, 1).char);\n}\n\ntest \"regression: Paragraph word wrap handles long words\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 5, 5);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    // Word longer than width - should hard wrap\n    const para = Paragraph{\n        .text = \"ABCDEFGH\",\n        .wrap = .word,\n    };\n    para.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 5, 5), &buf);\n\n    // Should hard wrap at width since no spaces\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'A'), buf.get(0, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'E'), buf.get(4, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'F'), buf.get(0, 1).char);\n}\n\ntest \"regression: Paragraph handles trailing newline\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 5);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    const para = Paragraph{ .text = \"Line1\\n\" };\n    para.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 5), &buf);\n\n    try style_mod.Style;\n\n/// Tabs widget displaying a horizontal tab bar.\n///\n/// Renders a row of tab titles with the selected tab highlighted.\n/// Tabs are separated by a configurable divider string.\npub const Tabs = struct {\n    /// Tab titles to display\n    titles: []const []const u8,\n\n    /// Index of the currently selected tab\n    selected: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Default style for unselected tabs\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Style for the selected tab\n    highlight_style: Style = Style.init().bold().fg(.yellow),\n\n    /// Divider string between tabs\n    divider: []const u8 = \" | \",\n\n    /// Render the tabs into the buffer at the given area.\n    /// Tabs are rendered horizontally on the first row of the area.\n    pub fn render(self: Tabs, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n        if (self.titles.len == 0) return;\n\n        var x = area.x;\n\n        for (self.titles, 0..) |title, idx| {\n            if (x >= area.right()) break;\n\n            // Determine if this tab is selected\n            const is_selected = idx == self.selected;\n            const tab_style = if (is_selected) self.highlight_style else self.style;\n\n            // Render tab title\n            const available_width = area.right() -| x;\n            if (available_width == 0) break;\n\n            const title_len = text_mod.displayWidth(title);\n            const render_len = @min(title_len, available_width);\n\n            if (render_len > 0) {\n                buf.setString(x, area.y, title, tab_style);\n            }\n\n            x +|= @intCast(render_len);\n\n            // Render divider after tab (except for last tab)\n            if (idx + 1 < self.titles.len and x < area.right()) {\n                const divider_available = area.right() -| x;\n                const divider_len = text_mod.displayWidth(self.divider);\n                const divider_render_len = @min(divider_len, divider_available);\n\n                if (divider_render_len > 0) {\n                    buf.setString(x, area.y, self.divider, self.style);\n                }\n\n                x +|= @intCast(divider_render_len);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get the number of tabs\n    pub fn count(self: Tabs) usize {\n        return self.titles.len;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if tabs are empty\n    pub fn isEmpty(self: Tabs) bool {\n        return self.titles.len == 0;\n    }\n\n    /// Get the selected tab index, clamped to valid range\n    pub fn selectedClamped(self: Tabs) ?usize {\n        if (self.titles.len == 0) return null;\n        return @min(self.selected, self.titles.len - 1);\n    }\n};\n\n\n// ============================================================\n// tabs.divider);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Tabs.count and Tabs.isEmpty\" {\n    const titles = [_][]const u8{ \"A\", \"B\" };\n    const tabs = Tabs{ .titles = &titles };\n\n    try {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 30, 3);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    const titles = [_][]const u8{ \"One\", \"Two\", \"Three\" };\n    const tabs = Tabs{\n        .titles =
